			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = PLX_PL_econ_depression_fiscal_2 }

					add_idea = PLX_PL_econ_depression_fiscal_2
				}
			}
			if = {

				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PLX_PL_econ_depression_fiscal_4
					add_idea = PLX_PL_econ_depression_fiscal_3
				}
			}

					remove_idea = PLX_PL_econ_depression_fiscal_5
					add_idea = PLX_PL_econ_depression_fiscal_4
				}
			}			

			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_idea = PLX_PL_econ_depression_5					
				}
				add_stability = -0.10
			}				
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = PLX_PL_econ_depression_4 }
				swap_ideas = {

					add_idea = PLX_PL_econ_depression_5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = PLX_PL_econ_depression_3 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PLX_PL_econ_depression_3
					add_idea = PLX_PL_econ_depression_4
				}
			}

					remove_idea = PLX_PL_econ_depression_2

				}

					remove_idea = PLX_PL_econ_depression_1
					add_idea = PLX_PL_econ_depression_2
				}
			}			
			if = {

				}
				else = {
					create_intelligence_agency = yes
				}

					limit = { has_idea = POL_dwojka_lar }

						remove_idea = POL_dwojka_lar
						add_idea = POL_dwojka_lar2
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_ideas = POL_dwojka_lar2
					add_political_power = -35
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = POL_dwojka }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = POL_dwojka
					add_idea = POL_dwojka2
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = POL_dwojka2
				add_political_power = -35
			}
		}

	}
